[30;1m1 | [0m[35mRemarks on Adaptation and Typecasting[0m
[30;1m2 | [0m[35m=====================================[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m.. currentmodule:: pg[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mBoth PostgreSQL and Python have the concept of data types, but there[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mare of course differences between the two type systems.  Therefore PyGreSQL[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mneeds to adapt Python objects to the representation required by PostgreSQL[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m121[0m[34m of [0m[33m411[0m[31m ]--[0m
